```#include <bits/stdc++.h>

using namespace std;

class A;

class B {
public:
    int get_a() const {
        return a;
    }

    friend class A;
private:
    int a = 0;
};

class A : public B {
public:
    void set_a(int b, B& a) {
        a.a = b;
    }
};

class C: public A{};

int main() {
    B b;
    C c;

    c.set_a(12, b);
    std::cout << b.get_a() << std::endl;
}```

```for (i = number.size(); static_cast<long>(i - bucket_length_) >
                                static_cast<long>(first_nonzero);
             i -= bucket_length_) {
            bucket =
                std::stoul(number.substr(i - bucket_length_, bucket_length_));
            digits.push_back(bucket);
        }
        if (i > static_cast<long>(first_nonzero)) {
            bucket =
                std::stoul(number.substr(first_nonzero, i - first_nonzero));
            digits.push_back(bucket);
        }```

```bigint(const std::string &number
    ) {  // cppcheck-suppress noExplicitConstructor
        const std::size_t first_nonzero = number.find_first_not_of('0');
        for (std::vector<unsigned int>::reverse_iterator i = digits.rbegin() - bucket_length_; i > digits.rend();
             i += bucket_length_) {
            std::size_t bucket_end = i - digits.rend();
            unsigned long bucket = std::stoul(number.substr(
                std::max(first_nonzero, bucket_end), bucket_length_
            ));
            digits.push_back(bucket);
        }
        digits.push_back(std::stoul(number.substr(
            first_nonzero, bucket_length_
        )));
        if (digits.empty()) {
            digits.push_back(0);
        }
    }
```

[2025-10-04T16:04:51+00:00] quassab:
Delegating constructor
If the name of the class itself appears as class-or-identifier in the member initializer list, then the list must consist of that one member initializer only; such a constructor is known as the delegating constructor, and the constructor selected by the only member of the initializer list is the target constructor.

In this case, the target constructor is selected by overload resolution and executed first, then the control returns to the delegating constructor and its body is executed.

Delegating constructors cannot be recursive.
--------------------------------------------------
